13/3/19 12:46 - David Betancur S: According the Oxford Dictionary of English, the word "woman" came from Old English wÄ«fmon, which has deep relation with the word "wife". The word "man" is of Germanic origin, and related to Dutch man, German Mann and Sanskrit manu. 

However, the word "human" is not of Germanic origin. The Latin word homo means "human", and its adjective form humanus means "of human" or "humane". The word went into Old French and become humain(e), and then went to late Middle English humaine, which eventually turns into the word "human" now. If you know French, you must know the word humain. It has the same origin with "human". 

From the etymology we can know that the two words are from Germanic origin and Roman origin respectively. They just own the part of "MAN" coincidentally.

Usually, the Roman origin words form their plurals by adding an "s". So the plural of the word "human" is "humans" instead of "humen".

def find_nearest(array, value):
    array = np.asarray(array)
    idx = (np.abs(array - value)).argmin()
    return idx

def graficar(nombregrafica, fecha,x1,y1,x2,y2,x3,y3,toh):
    nombre = nombregrafica
    n = 1

    while os.path.isfile(nombre + "_" + fecha + '.html'):
        nombre = nombregrafica + '_(' + str(n) + ')'
        n += 1

    titulo = 'Calibracion ' + nombregrafica
    n1 = 'Camara'
    n2 = 'Sensor'
    n3 = 'Ajuste'

    x1 = np.array(x1).reshape((1, -1))[0]
    x2 = np.array(x2).reshape((1, -1))[0]
    x3 = np.array(x3).reshape((1, -1))[0]
    y1 = np.array(y1).reshape((1, -1))[0]
    y2 = np.array(y2).reshape((1, -1))[0]
    y3 = np.array(y3).reshape((1, -1))[0]

    trace1 = go.Scatter(x=x1, y=y1, name=n1, marker=dict(color='blue'))
    trace2 = go.Scatter(x=x2, y=y2, name=n2, yaxis='y', marker=dict(color='orange'))
    trace3 = go.Scatter(x=x3, y=y3, name=n3, yaxis='y', marker=dict(color='green'))

    data = [trace1, trace2, trace3]

    layout = go.Layout(
        title=titulo,
        # width=1800,
        xaxis=dict(
            title='Tiempo (h)',
            # showticklabels=True,
            # domain=[0.03, 0.94]
        ),
        yaxis=dict(
            # title='Variable',
            showticklabels=True,
            titlefont=dict(color='blue'),
            tickfont=dict(color='blue')
        ),
        yaxis2=dict(
            # title='yaxis2 title',
            showticklabels=True,
            titlefont=dict(color='orange'),
            tickfont=dict(color='orange'),
            anchor='free',
            overlaying='y',
            side='left',
            # position=0.0
        ),
        yaxis3=dict(
            # title='yaxis4 title',
            showticklabels=True,
            titlefont=dict(color='green'),
            tickfont=dict(color='green'),
            anchor='x',
            overlaying='y',
            side='right'
        )
    )

    fig = go.Figure(data=data, layout=layout)
    if toh==1:
        plotly.offline.plot(fig, filename="D:\Documentos\PIMEDICA\Calibracion_sensores\sensores\Regresion\\resultados_ajustes\\Humedad_Graf_" + nombre + "_" + fecha + '.html')
    elif toh==2:
        plotly.offline.plot(fig, filename="D:\Documentos\PIMEDICA\Calibracion_sensores\sensores\Regresion\\resultados_ajustes\\Temperatura_Graf_" + nombre + "_" + fecha + '.html')
    elif toh == 3:
        plotly.offline.plot(fig, filename="D:\Documentos\PIMEDICA\Calibracion_sensores\sensores\Regresion\\resultados_ajustes\\Sonda_Graf_" + nombre + "_" + fecha + '.html')
    elif toh == 4:
        plotly.offline.plot(fig, filename="D:\Documentos\PIMEDICA\Calibracion_sensores\sensores\Regresion\\resultados_ajustes\\Camara_cruda_Graf_" + nombre + "_" + fecha + '.html')
    elif toh ==5:
        titulo = 'Regresion Temp ' + nombregrafica

        trace1 = go.Scatter(x=x1, y=y1, name=n1,mode = 'markers', marker=dict(color='blue'))
        data = [trace1, trace2, trace3]
        layout = go.Layout(
            title=titulo,
            # width=1800,
            xaxis=dict(
                title='Temperatura camara',
                # showticklabels=True,
                # domain=[0.03, 0.94]
            ),
            yaxis=dict(
                title='Temperatura sensor',
